INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
ACQUISTION OF LANDS
 FORM - VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-III, Blocks 1-8
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡.203 ªî£N™ (Tä‹)ˆ ¶¬ø 25 Ýèv† 2021, ÝõE 9, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2052]
No. II(2)/IND/583(b-1)/2021.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 226.94.10 hectares of land is required in the Padukkapathu 
and Pallakurichi Villages in Sathankulam Taluk in Thoothukudi District for a public purpose, namely, in establishing 
a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 97.31.11 hectares in Block-1 to 8, 
Unit-III is under acquisition for the above said project in the Padukkapathu and Pallakurichi Villages in Sathankulam 
Taluk in Thoothukudi District whose detailed description is as follows:
[ 1 ]

This declaration is made under Section 19(1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land 
Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project aﬀ ected family in Block No.1 to 8 of Unit-III and hence 
the Elements of rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to 
Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply.
 Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
 A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
 
 
                                          N. MURUGANANDAM,
 
                                          Principal Secretary to Government.

FORM - VI
DECLARATION
UNIT-IV, BLOCK 1-10
[murhiz (ãiy) v©. 204, bjhêš (í.I.v«), 25 Mf°£ 2021, Mtâ 9, Ãyt,
 ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052]
No. II(2)/IND/583(b-2)/2021.
    Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 217.04.90 hectares of land is required in the Padukkapathu Village in Sathankulam Taluk in Thoothukkudi 
District for a public purpose, namely, in establishing a new launch station for SSLV in favour of ISRO and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 112.33.30 hectares in Block 1 to 10, Unit-IV is under acquisition for 
the above said project in the Padukkapathu Village in Sathankulam Taluk in Thoothukkudi District whose detailed description is as follows:

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
161
This declaration is made under Section 19(1) read with sub-section (4) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, 
Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). There is no project affected family in Block No.1 to 8 of Unit-III and hence the Elements of 
rehabilitation and resettlement entitlements under Second Schedule and provision of infrastructural amenities under Third Schedule of Right to Fair Compensation and 
Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) shall not apply.
 Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
 A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Land Acquisition officer / District Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Officer 
(L.A), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur on any working day.
N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary To Government.
